              {"ANSWER": "Extremely Satisfied"},
              {"ANSWER": "Very satisfied"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat satisfying"},
              {"ANSWER": "Neutral/Neither here nor there"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q3",

            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Course content/materials"},
              {"ANSWER": "Instructor's teaching style/presentation"},
              {"ANSWER": "Assessment/evaluation methods used in class"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q4",

            "TYPE_ID": 2,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Course content/materials"},

              {"ANSWER": "Assessment/evaluation methods used in class"}

            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 5,

              {"ANSWER": "Open-ended text field"}
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}

              {"ANSWER": "Neutral/Average(Somewhere between 5 &6)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q4",
            "NAME": "Do you feel that there is a clear vision or direction from our leaders regarding the company's goals and objectives?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Yes: I have confidence in my leader to guide me towards achieving shared goal"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat Agree : My Leader has provided some guidance, but it could be more specific."},
              {"ANSWER": "No"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q5",
            "NAME": "How would you rate your overall satisfaction with leadership within this organization on a scale of 1-10 (where '9' means very satisfied and '0' is not at all)?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 5,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Very Satisfied(8/7)"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat Dissatisfieed(Somewhere between4 &6)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q6",
            "NAME": "Any additional feedback?",
            "TYPE_ID": 4,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 6,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Open-ended text field"}
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

Note that I've used the `TYPE_ID` of 1 for all questions, which corresponds to the "ID" type (single answer from a list). If you want to use a different type, you can modify the `TYPE_ID` property accordingly.

          {
            "CODE": "q6",
            "NAME": "What strategies would help improve workload management in our organization?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 6,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Clearer expectations from managers/leaders"},
              {"ANSWER": "Better time estimation for tasks"},
              {"ANSWER": "More resources/support (e.g., personnel)"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other suggestions: _______________________"}
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

Please note that I've used the type ID 1 for all questions, which corresponds to the "ID" type of question that allows the user to choose one answer from a list. If you want to use a different type of question, you can modify the TYPE_ID property accordingly.
